Overview\n     </h1>\n     <!-- jade cannot include dynamically-->\n     <p>\n      <strong>\n       Angular-xeditable\n      </strong>\n      is a bundle of\n      <a href="http://angularjs.org">\n       AngularJS\n      </a>\n      directives that allows you to create\n      <em>\n       editable elements\n      </em>\n      .\nSuch technique is also known as\n      <em>\n       click-to-edit\n      </em>\n      or\n      <em>\n       edit-in-place\n      </em>\n      .\nIt is based on ideas of\n      <a href="http://vitalets.github.io/x-editable">\n       x-editable\n      </a>\n      but was written from scratch\nto use power of angular and support complex forms / editable grids.\n     </p>\n     <h4>\n      Dependencies\n     </h4>\n     <p>\n      Basically it does not depend on any libraries except\n      <a href="http://angularjs.org">\n       AngularJS\n      </a>\n      itself.\nFor themes you may need to include\n      <a href="http://getbootstrap.com">\n       Twitter Bootstrap\n      </a>\n      CSS.\nFor some extra controls (e.g. datepicker) you may need to include\n      <a href="http://angular-ui.github.io/bootstrap/">\n       angular-ui bootstrap\n      </a>\n      for Bootstrap 2/3.\nInclude\n      <a href="https://morgul.github.io/ui-bootstrap4/">\n       ui-bootstrap4\n      </a>\n      for Bootstrap 4.\nFor ui-select you may need to include\n      <a href="https://github.com/angular-ui/ui-select/">\n       angular-ui ui-select\n      </a>\n      .\nFor ngTagsInput you may need to include\n      <a href="https://github.com/mbenford/ngTagsInput">\n       mbenford ngTagsInput\n      </a>\n      .\nIf installing via NPM, jQuery and moment js will also be installed.\n     </p>\n     <h4>\n      Controls &amp; Features\n     </h4>\n     <table style="width: 50%; min-width: 200px">\n      <tbody>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="width: 50%; vertical-align: top">\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#text-simple">\n            text\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#textarea">\n            textarea\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#select-local">\n            select\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#checklist">\n            checkbox\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#radiolist">\n            radio\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#bsdate">\n            date\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#bstime">\n            time\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#combodate">\n            datetime\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#html5-inputs">\n            html5 inputs\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#typeahead">\n            typeahead\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#uiselect">\n            ui-select\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#ngtags">\n            ngTagsInput\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td style="width: 50%; vertical-align: top">\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#editable-form">\n            complex form\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#editable-row">\n            editable row\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#editable-column">\n            editable column\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#editable-table">\n            editable table\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <a href="#themes">\n            themes\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </tbody>\n     </table>\n     <section id="getstarted">\n     </section>\n     <h1>\n      Get started\n     </h1>\n     <!-- jade cannot include dynamically-->\n     <ol>\n      <li>\n       <p>\n        Include\n        <a href="http://angularjs.org">\n         Angular.js\n        </a>\n        in your project\n       </p>\n       <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="tag">&lt;script</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">src</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"https://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/angularjs/1.5.0/angular.min.js"</span><span class="tag">&gt;&lt;/script&gt;</span></pre>\n       <p>\n        Optionally include\n        <a href="http://getbootstrap.com">\n         Bootstrap\n        </a>\n        CSS for theming\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        Bootstrap 3\n       </p>\n       <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="tag">&lt;link</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">href</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"https://netdna.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.6/css/bootstrap.min.css"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">rel</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"stylesheet"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span></pre>\n       <p>\n        Boostrap 4\n       </p>\n       <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="tag">&lt;link</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">href</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"https://stackpath.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/4.3.1/css/bootstrap.min.css"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">rel</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"stylesheet"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span></pre>\n      </li>\n      <li>\n       <span>\n        Install angular-xeditable via\n       </span>\n       <a href="http://bower.io" target="_blank">\n        bower\n       </a>\n       <span>\n        or\n       </span>\n       <a href="zip/angular-xeditable-0.10.0.zip">\n        download latest zip\n       </a>\n       <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="pln">bower install angular</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln">xeditable</span></pre>\n      </li>\n      <li>\n       Include angular-xeditable into your project\n       <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="tag">&lt;link</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">href</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"bower_components/angular-xeditable/dist/css/xeditable.css"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">rel</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"stylesheet"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span><span class="pln">\n</span><span class="tag">&lt;script</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">src</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"bower_components/angular-xeditable/dist/js/xeditable.js"</span><span class="tag">&gt;&lt;/script&gt;</span></pre>\n      </li>\n      <li>\n       Define angular app and add "xeditable" to dependencies\n       <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="tag">&lt;html</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">ng-app</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"app"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span></pre>\n       <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="kwd">var</span><span class="pln"> app </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> angular</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="kwd">module</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"app"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">[</span><span class="str">"xeditable"</span><span class="pun">]);</span></pre>\n      </li>\n      <li>\n       Set theme in app.run:\n       <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="pln">app</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">run</span><span class="pun">([</span><span class="str">\'editableOptions\'</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">function</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">editableOptions</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">\n  editableOptions</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">theme </span><span <script>\n       app.controller(\'SelectRemoteCtrl\', function($scope, $filter, $http) {\n  $scope.user = {\n    group: 4,\n    groupName: \'admin\' // original value\n  }; \n\n  $scope.groups = [];\n\n  $scope.loadGroups = function() {\n    return $scope.groups.length ? null : $http.get(\'/groups\').success(function(data) {\n      $scope.groups = data;\n    });\n  };\n\n  $scope.$watch(\'user.group\', function(newVal, oldVal) {\n    if (newVal !== oldVal) {\n      var selected = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.groups, {id: $scope.user.group});\n      $scope.user.groupName = selected.length ? selected[0].text : null;\n    }\n  });\n$scope.$watch("user", function(v) { $scope.$parent.debug["select-remote"]=v; }); });\n      </script>\n      <h3>\n       html\n      </h3>\n <h1>\n       Checklist\n      </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <div class="well line-example">\n       <div class="ng-scope" ng-controller="ChecklistCtrl">\n        <a class="ng-scope ng-binding editable editable-click" e-ng-disabled="disableCheckbox(s.value)" e-ng-options="s.value as s.text for s in statuses" editable-checklist="user.status" href="#">\n         status2, status3\n        </a>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <pre class="ng-binding">{\n  "status": [\n    2,\n    3\n  ]\n}</pre>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       To create list of checkboxes use\n       <code>\n        editable-checklist\n       </code>\n       attribute pointing to model.\nAlso you should define\n       <code>\n        e-ng-options\n       </code>\n       attribute to set value and display items.\nOptionally define\n       <code>\n        e-checklist-comparator\n       </code>\n       to use a function to determine which checkboxes are actually checked.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <strong>\n        Please note\n       </strong>\n       , you should include\n       <a href="http://vitalets.github.io/checklist-model">\n        checklist-model directive\n       </a>\n       into your app:\n       <code>\n        var app = angular.module("app", [..., "checklist-model"]);\n       </code>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       To disable a checkbox include the attribute\n       <code>\n        e-ng-disabled\n       </code>\n       and pass a condition.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       By default, checkboxes aligned\n       <em>\n        horizontally\n       </em>\n       . To align\n       <em>\n        vertically\n       </em>\n       just add following\n       <strong>\n        CSS\n       </strong>\n       :\n      </p>\n      <pre><code>.editable-checklist label {\n  display: block;\n}</code></pre>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <!--script(src=dir+\'/controller.js\')-->\n      <script>\n       app.controller(\'ChecklistCtrl\', function($scope, $filter) {\n  $scope.user = {\n    status: [2, 3]\n  };\n\n  $scope.statuses = [\n    {value: 1, text: \'status1\'},\n    {value: 2, text: \'status2\'},\n    {value: 3, text: \'status3\'}\n  ];\n\n  $scope.showStatus = function() {\n    var selected = [];\n    angular.forEach($scope.statuses, function(s) {\n      if ($scope.user.status.indexOf(s.value) >= 0) {\n        selected.push(s.text);\n      }\n    });\n    return selected.length ? selected.join(\', \') : \'Not set\';\n  };\n\n  $scope.disableCheckbox = function (v) {\n    if ($scope.user.status.indexOf(v) === -1) {\n      return true\n <section id="uidate">\n      <h1>\n       UI Date\n      </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <div class="well       11/04/1985\n        </span>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <pre class="ng-binding">{\n  "dob": "1985-04-10T23:00:00.000Z"\n}</pre>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Date control is Editable ui-bootstrap Popover\n      </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <div class="well line-example">\n       <div class="ng-scope" id="UiPopoverCtrl" ng-controller="UiPopoverCtrl">\n        <div class="ui-popover-wrapper">\n         <a class="ng-scope ng-binding editable editable-click" e-label="User Name" editable-text="user.name" href="#" id="simpleText" onhide="popoverIsOpen = !popoverIsOpen" onshow="popoverIsOpen = !popoverIsOpen" popover="true" popover-append-to-body="true" popover-is-open="popoverIsOpen" uib-popover-template="\'popover.html\'">\n          awesome user\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <pre class="ng-binding">{\n  "name": "awesome user",\n  "location": "location 1"\n}</pre>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       To make a single element editable via\n       <code>\n        ui-boostrap popover\n       </code>\n       do the following:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Wrap the editable in\n        <code>\n         &lt;div class="ui-popover-wrapper"&gt;\n        </code>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Put the following attributes on the editable element:\n        <ul>\n         <li>\n          <code>\n           uib-popover-template="\'popover.html\'"\n          </code>\n          - The template is generated when the\n          <code>\n           popover\n          </code>\n          attribute is set to `true\'\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <code>\n           popover-is-open="popoverIsOpen"\n          </code>\n          - Controls when the popover is opened\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <code>\n           onshow="popoverIsOpen = !popoverIsOpen"\n          </code>\n          - Opens the popover when the editable form is shown\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <code>\n           onhide="popoverIsOpen = !popoverIsOpen"\n          </code>\n          - Closes the popover when the editable form is closed\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <code>\n           popover="true"\n          </code>\n          - Tells the editable directive that this element is to be displayed in the ui-bootstrap popover\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n id="e-single">\n      <h1>\n       Single editable in a form\n      </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <div class="well line-example">\n       <div class="ng-scope" id="ESingleCtrl" ng-controller="ESingleCtrl">\n        <form class="ng-pristine ng-valid">\n         <a class="ng-scope ng-binding editable editable-click" e-single="" editable-text="user.name" href="#">\n          awesome user\n         </a>\n        </form>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <pre class="ng-binding">{\n  "name": "awesome user"\n}</pre>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Add\n       <code>\n        e-single\n       </code>\n       attribute when you want a single item to be clickable inside of a form.\n       <br/>\n       It ignores the outer form.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <!--script(src=dir+\'/controller.js\')-->\n      <script>\n       app.controller(\'ESingleCtrl\',    </h3>\n      <pre class="prettyprint ng-non-bindable prettyprinted" style=""><span class="tag">&lt;div</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">ng-controller</span><span    Submit via onbeforesave\n      </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <a class="btn btn-info fiddle pull-right" href="http://jsfiddle.net/ckosloski/NfPcH/19056/" target="_blank">\n       jsFiddle\n      </a>\n      <div class="well line-example">\n       <div class="ng-scope" id="OnbeforesaveCtrl" ng-controller="OnbeforesaveCtrl">\n        <a class="ng-scope ng-binding editable editable-click" editable-text="user.name" href="#" onbeforesave="updateUser($data)">\n         awesome user\n        </a>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <pre class="ng-binding">{\n  "id": 1,\n  "name": "awesome user"\n}</pre>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       One way to submit data on server is to define\n       <code>\n        onbeforesave\n       </code>\n       attribute pointing to some method of scope.\nUseful when you need to send data on server first and only then update local model (e.g.\n       <code>\n        $scope.user\n       </code>\n       ).\nNew value can be passed as\n       <code>\n        $data\n       </code>\n       parameter (e.g.\n       <code>\n        &lt;a ... onbeforesave="updateUser($data)"&gt;\n       </code>\n       ).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The main thing is that local model will be updated only if method returns\n       <code>\n        true\n       </code>\n       or\n       <code>\n        undefined\n       </code>\n       (or promise resolved to\n       <code>\n        true/undefined\n       </code>\n       ). Commonly there are 3 cases depending on result type:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         true\n        </code>\n        or\n        <code>\n         undefined\n        </code>\n        : \nSuccess. Local model will be updated automatically and form will close.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         false\n        </code>\n        : \nSuccess. But local model will\n        <strong>\n         not\n        </strong>\n        be updated and form will close. Useful when you want to update local model manually (e.g. server changed values).\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         string\n        </code>\n        : \nError. Local model will\n        <strong>\n         not\n        </strong>\n        be updated, form will\n        <strong>\n         not\n        </strong>\n        close, string will be shown as error message.\nUseful for validation and processing errors.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <!--script(src=dir+\'/controller.js\')-->\n      <script>\n       app.controller(\'OnbeforesaveCtrl\', function($scope, $http) {\n  $scope.user = {\n    id: 1,\n    name: \'awesome user\'\n  };\n\n  $scope.updateUser = function(data) {\n    return $http.post(\'/updateUser\', {id: $scope.user.id, name: data});\n  };\n$scope.$watch("user", function(v) { $scope.$parent.debug["onbeforesave"]=v; }); });\n      </script>\n      <h3>\n       html\n      </h3>\n      <pre class="prettyprint ng-non-bindable prettyprinted" style=""><span class="tag">&lt;div</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">ng-controller</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"OnbeforesaveCtrl"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">id</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"OnbeforesaveCtrl"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span><span class="pln">\n  </span><span class="tag">&lt;a</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">href</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"#"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">editable-text</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"user.name"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">onbeforesave</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"</span><span class="pln">updateUser</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">$data</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="atv">"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span><span class="pln">\n    {{ user.name || \'empty\' }}\n  </span><span class="tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="pln">\n</span><span class="tag">&lt;/div&gt;</span></pre>\n      <h3>\n       controller.js\n      </h3>\n      <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="pln">app</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">controller</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">\'OnbeforesaveCtrl\'</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">function</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">user </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">\n    id</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln">\n    name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">\'awesome user\'</span><span class="pln">\n  </span><span class="pun">};</span><span class="pln">\n\n  $scope</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">updateUser </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">function</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">data</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">\n    </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> $http</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">post</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">\'/updateUser\'</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">id</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> $scope</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">user</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">id</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> data</span><span class="pun">});</span><span class="pln">\n  </span><span class="pun">};</span><span class="pln">\n</span><span class="pun">});</span></pre>\n     </section>\n     <section id="onaftersave">\n      <h1>\n       Submit via onaftersave\n      </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <a class="btn btn-info fiddle pull-right" href="http://jsfiddle.net/ckosloski/NfPcH/19057/" target="_blank">\n       jsFiddle\n      </a>\n      <div class="well line-example">\n       <div class="ng-scope" id="OnaftersaveCtrl" ng-controller="OnaftersaveCtrl">\n        <a class="ng-scope ng-binding editable editable-click" editable-text="user.name" href="#" onaftersave="updateUser()">\n         awesome user\n        </a>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <pre class="ng-binding">{\n  "id": 1,\n  "name": "awesome user"\n}</pre>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Another way to submit data on server is to define\n       <code>\n        onaftersave\n       </code>\n       attribute pointing to some method of scope.\nUseful when you need to update local model first and only then send it to server.\nThere are no input parameters as data already in local model.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The result type of this method can be following:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        anything except\n        <code>\n         string\n        </code>\n        : success, form will be closed\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         string\n        </code>\n        : error, form will\n        <strong>\n         not\n        </strong>\n        close, string will be shown as error message\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       Note that you can use both\n       <code>\n        onbeforesave\n       </code>\n       for validation and\n       <code>\n        onaftersave\n       </code>\n       for saving data.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <!--script(src=dir+\'/controller.js\')-->\n      <script>\n       app.controller(\'OnaftersaveCtrl\', function($scope, $http) {\n  $scope.user = {\n    id: 1,\n    name: \'awesome user\'\n  };\n\n  $scope.updateUser = function() {\n    return $http.post(\'/updateUser\', $scope.user);\n  };\n$scope.$watch("user", function(v) { $scope.$parent.debug["onaftersave"]=v; }); });\n      </script>\n      <h3>\n       html\n      </h3>\n      <pre class="prettyprint ng-non-bindable prettyprinted" style=""><span class="tag">&lt;div</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">ng-controller</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"OnaftersaveCtrl"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">id</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"OnaftersaveCtrl"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span><span class="pln">\n  </span><span class="tag">&lt;a</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">href</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"#"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">editable-text</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"user.name"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">onaftersave</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"</span><span class="pln">updateUser</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="atv">"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span><span class="pln">\n    {{ user.name || \'empty\' }}\n  </span><span class="tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="pln">\n</span><span class="tag">&lt;/div&gt;</span></pre>\n      <h3>\n       controller.js\n      </h3>\n      <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><span class="pln">app</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">controller</span><span class="pln">$scope</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> $http</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">\n  $scope</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">user </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">\n    id</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln">\n    name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">\'awesome user\'</span><span class="pln">\n  </span><span class="pun">};</span><span class="pln">\n\n  $scope</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">updateUser </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> $http</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">post</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">\'/updateUser\'</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> $scope</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">user</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">\n  </span><span class="pun">};</span><span class="pln">\n</span><span class="pun">});</span></pre>\n     </section>\n     <section id="editable-form">\n      <h1>\n       Editable form\n      </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <a class="btn btn-info fiddle pull-right" href="http://jsfiddle.net/ckosloski/NfPcH/19058/" target="_blank">\n       jsFiddle\n      </a>\n      <div class="well line-example">\n       <div class="ng-scope" id="EditableFormCtrl" ng-controller="EditableFormCtrl">\n        <form class="ng-pristine ng-valid" editable-form="" name="editableForm" onaftersave="saveUser()">\n         <div>\n          <!-- editable username (text with validation) -->\n          <span class="title">\n           User name:\n          </span>\n          <span class="ng-scope ng-binding editable" e-name="name" e-required="" editable-text="user.name" onbeforesave="checkName($data)">\n           awesome user\n          </span>\n         </div>\n         <div>\n          <!-- editable status (select-local) -->\n          <span class="title">\n           Status:\n          </span>\n          <span class="ng-scope ng-binding editable" e-name="status" e-ng-options="s.value as s.text for s in statuses" editable-select="user.status">\n           status2\n          </span>\n         </div>\n         <div>\n          <!-- editable group (select-remote) -->\n          <span class="title">\n           Group:\n          </span>\n          <span class="ng-scope ng-binding editable" e-name="group" e-ng-options="g.id as g.text for g in groups" editable-select="user.group" onshow="loadGroups()">\n           admin\n          </span>\n         </div>\n         <div class="buttons">\n          <!-- button to show form -->\n          <button class="btn btn-default" ng-click="editableForm.$show()" ng-show="!editableForm.$visible" type="button">\n           Edit\n          </button>\n          <!-- buttons to submit / cancel form -->\n          <span class="ng-hide" ng-show="editableForm.$visible">\n           <button class="btn btn-primary" ng-disabled="editableForm.$waiting" type="submit">\n            Save\n           </button>\n           <button class="btn btn-default" ng-click="editableForm.$cancel()" ng-disabled="editableForm.$waiting" type="button">\n            Cancel\n           </button>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </form>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       To show several editable elements together and submit at once you should wrap them into\n       <code>\n        &lt;form editable-form name="myform" ...&gt;\n       </code>\n       tag. The\n       <code>\n        name\n       </code>\n       attribute of form will create variable in scope (normal angular behavior) and\n       <code>\n        editable-form\n       </code>\n       attribute will add a few methods to that variable:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        $show()\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        $cancel()\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        $visible\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        $waiting\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       Use it to toggle editable state of form. For example, you can call\n       <code>\n        myform.$show()\n       </code>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Editable form supports 3 additional attributes:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <strong>\n         onshow\n        </strong>\n        : called when form is shown\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <strong>\n         onbeforesave\n        </strong>\n        : called on submit before local models update\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <strong>\n         onaftersave\n        </strong>\n        : called on submit after local models update\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       They work nearly the same as for individual editable elements. Use it instead of\n       <code>\n        ng-submit / submit\n       </code>\n       to get more control over saving process.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       When you submit editable form it performs following steps:\n      </p>\n      <ol>\n       <li>\n        call child\'s\n        <code>\n         onbeforesave\n        </code>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        call form\'s\n        <code>\n         onbeforesave\n        </code>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        write data to local model (e.g.\n        <code>\n         $scope.user\n        </code>\n        )\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        call form\'s\n        <code>\n         onaftersave\n        </code>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        call child\'s\n        <code>\n         onaftersave\n        </code>\n       </li>\n      </ol>\n      <p>\n       Any\n       <code>\n        onbeforesave / onaftersave\n       </code>\n       can be omited so in simplest case you will just write data to local model.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       But in more complex case it becomes usefull:\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       If you need\n       <strong>\n        validation of individual editable elements\n       </strong>\n       then you should define\n       <code>\n        onbeforesave\n       </code>\n       on particular editable element.\n       <br/>\n       The result of child\'s\n       <code>\n        onbeforesave\n       </code>\n       is important for next step:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         string\n        </code>\n        : submit will be cancelled, form will stay opened, string will be shown as error message\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         not string\n        </code>\n        : submit will be continued\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       If you need to\n       <strong>\n        send data on server\n        <em>\n         before\n        </em>\n        writing to local model\n       </strong>\n       then you should define form\'s\n       <code>\n        onbeforesave\n       </code>\n       .\n       <br/>\n       The result of form\'s\n       <code>\n        onbeforesave\n       </code>\n       is important for next step:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         true\n        </code>\n        or\n        <code>\n         undefined\n        </code>\n        : local model will be updated and form will call\n        <code>\n         onaftersave\n        </code>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         false\n        </code>\n        : local model\n        <strong>\n         will not be updated\n        </strong>\n        and form will just close (e.g. you update local model yourself)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         string\n        </code>\n        : local model\n        <strong>\n         will not be updated\n        </strong>\n        and\n        <strong>\n         form will not close\n        </strong>\n        (e.g. server error)\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       If you need to\n       <strong>\n        send data on server\n        <em>\n         after\n        </em>\n        writing to local model\n       </strong>\n       then you should define form\'s\n       <code>\n        onaftersave\n       </code>\n       .\n       <br/>\n       The result of form\'s\n       <code>\n        onaftersave\n       </code>\n       is also important for next step:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         string\n        </code>\n        : form will not close (e.g. server error)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code>\n         not string\n        </code>\n        : form will be closed\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       Commonly you should define\n       <code>\n        onbeforesave\n       </code>\n       for child elements to perform validation and\n       <code>\n        onaftersave\n       </code>\n       for whole form to send data on server.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Note:\n       <code>\n        e-required\n       </code>\n       will not work since HTML5 validation only works if submitting a form with a submit button and\n       <code>\n        editable-form\n       </code>\n       submits via a script.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Please have a look at examples.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <!--script(src=dir+\'/controller.js\')-->\n      <script>\n       app.controller(\'EditableFormCtrl\', function($scope, $filter, $http) {\n  $scope.user = {\n    id: 1,\n    name: \'awesome user\',\n    status: 2,\n    group: 4,\n    groupName: \'admin\'\n  }; \n\n  $scope.statuses = [\n    {value: 1, text: \'status1\'},\n    {value: 2, text: \'status2\'},\n    {value: 3, text: \'status3\'},\n    {value: 4, text: \'status4\'}\n  ]; \n\n  $scope.groups = [];\n  $scope.loadGroups = function() {\n    return $scope.groups.length ? null : $http.get(\'/groups\').success(function(data) {\n      $scope.groups = data;\n    });\n  };\n\n  $scope.showGroup = function() {\n    if($scope.groups.length) {\n      var selected = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.groups, {id: $scope.user.group});\n      return selected.length ? selected[0].text : \'Not set\';\n    } else {\n      return $scope.user.groupName;\n    }\n  };\n\n  $scope.checkName = function(data) {\n    if (data !== \'awesome\' && data !== \'error\') {\n      return "Username should be `awesome` or `error`";\n    }\n  };\n\n  $scope.saveUser = function() {\n    // $scope.user already updated!\n    return $http.post(\'/saveUser\', $scope.user).error(function(err) {\n      if(err.field && err.msg) {\n        // err like {field: "name", msg: "Server-side error for this username!"} \n        $scope.editableForm.$setError(err.field, err.msg);\n      } else { \n        // unknown error\n        $scope.editableForm.$setError(\'name\', \'Unknown error!\');\n      }\n    });\n  };\n});\n      </script>\n      <h3>\n       html\n      </h3>\n      <pre class="prettyprint   </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <a class="btn btn-info fiddle pull-right"       <table class="table table-bordered table-hover table-condensed">\n         <tbody>\n          <tr style="font-weight: bold">\n           <td style="width:35%">\n            Name\n editable elements in cells with\n       <code>\n        e-form\n       </code>\n       attribute pointing to form\'s name. The form itself can appear later (e.g. in last column) but it will work. Don\'t forget to add\n       <code>\n        editable-form\n       </code>\n       attribute to the form. The form behavior is absolutely the same as described in\n       <a href="#editable-form">\n        Editable form section\n       </a>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <!--script(src=dir+\'/controller.js\')-->\n      <script>\n       app.controller(\'EditableRowCtrl\', function($scope, $filter, $http) {\n  $scope.users = [\n    {id: 1, name: \'awesome user1\', \n\n  $scope.statuses = [\n    {value: 1, text: \'status1\'},\n    {value: 2, text: \'status2\'},\n    {value: 3, text: \'status3\'},\n    {value: 4, text: \'status4\'}\n  ]; \n\n  $scope.groups = [];\n  $scope.loadGroups = function() {\n    return $scope.groups.length ? null : $http.get(\'/groups\').success(function(data) {\n      $scope.groups = data;\n    });\n  };\n\n  $scope.showGroup = function(user) {\n    if(user.group && $scope.groups.length) {\n      var selected = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.groups, {id: user.group});\n      return selected.length ? selected[0].text : \'Not set\';\n    } else {\n      return user.groupName || \'Not set\';\n    }\n  };\n\n  $scope.showStatus = function(user) {\n    var selected = [];\n    if(user.status) {\n      selected = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.statuses, {value: user.status});\n    }\n    return selected.length ? selected[0].text : \'Not set\';\n  };\n\n  $scope.checkName = function(data, id) {\n    if (id === 2 && data !== \'awesome\') {\n      return "Username 2 should be `awesome`";\n    }\n  };\n\n  $scope.saveUser = function(data, id) {\n    //$scope.user not updated yet\n    angular.extend(data, {id: id});\n    return $http.post(\'/saveUser\', data);\n  };\n\n  // remove user\n  $scope.removeUser = function(index) {\n    $scope.users.splice(index, 1);\n  };\n\n  // add user\n  $scope.addUser = function() {\n    $scope.inserted = {\n      id: $scope.users.length+1,\n      name: \'\',\n      status: null,\n      group: null \n    };\n    $scope.users.push($scope.inserted);\n  };\n});\n <section id="editable-column">\n      <h1>\n       Editable column\n      </h1>\n      <!-- watch change of user to update rootScope for debugging-->\n      <h3>\n       demo\n      </h3>\n      <a class="btn btn-info fiddle pull-right" href="http://jsfiddle.net/ckosloski/NfPcH/19060/" target="_blank">\n       jsFiddle\n      </a>\n      <div class="well line-example">\n       <div class="ng-scope" ng-controller="EditableColumnCtrl">\n        <table class="table table-bordered table-hover table-condensed">\n         <tbody>\n          <tr style="font-weight: bold; white-space: nowrap">\n           <!-- username header -->\n           <td style="width:40%">\n            Name\n            <form class="ng-pristine ng-valid ng-hide" editable-form="" name="nameform" ng-show="nameform.$visible" onaftersave="saveColumn(\'name\')">\n             <button class="btn btn-primary" ng-disabled="nameform.$waiting" type="submit">\n              save\n             </button>\n             <button class="btn btn-default" ng-click="nameform.$cancel()" ng-disabled="nameform.$waiting" type="button">\n              cancel\n             </button>\n            </form>\n            <button class="btn btn-default" ng-click="nameform.$show()" ng-show="!nameform.$visible">\n             edit\n            </button>\n           </td>\n           <!-- status        <button class="btn btn-primary" ng-disabled="groupform.$waiting" type="submit">\n              save\n             </button>\n             <button class="btn btn-default" e-name="name" editable-text="user.name" onbeforesave="checkName($data)">\n             awesome user1\n            </span>\n           </td>\n           <td>\n            <!-- editable status       status2\n            </span>\n           </td>\n           <td>\n            <!-- editable group (select-remote) -->\n            <span class="ng-scope ng-binding editable" e-form="groupform"      </table>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       To create editable column in table you should place editable elements in cells with\n       <code>\n        e-form\n       </code>\n       attribute pointing to form\'s name. The form itself can appear in column header or footer. The form behavior is absolutely the same as described in\n       <a href="#editable-form">\n        Editable form section\n       </a>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <!--script(src=dir+\'/controller.js\')-->\n      <script>\n       app.controller(\'EditableColumnCtrl\', function($scope, $filter, $http, $q) {\n  $scope.users = [\n    {id: 1, name: \'awesome user1\', status: 2, group: 4, groupName: \'admin\'},\n    {id: 2, name: \'awesome user2\', status: undefined, group: 3, groupName: \'vip\'},\n    {id: 3, name: \'awesome user3\', status: 2, group: null}\n  ]; \n\n  $scope.statuses = [\n    {value: 1, text: \'status1\'},\n    {value: 2, text: \'status2\'},\n    {value: 3, text: \'status3\'},\n    {value: 4, text: \'status4\'}\n  ]; \n\n  $scope.groups = [];\n  $scope.loadGroups = function() {\n    return $scope.groups.length ? null : $http.get(\'/groups\').success(function(data) {\n      $scope.groups = data;\n    });\n  };\n\n  $scope.showGroup = function(user) {\n    if(user.group && $scope.groups.length) {\n      var selected = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.groups, {id: user.group});\n      return selected.length ? selected[0].text : \'Not set\';\n    } else {\n      return user.groupName || \'Not set\';\n    }\n  };\n\n  $scope.showStatus = function(user) {\n    var selected = [];\n    if(user.status) {\n      selected = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.statuses, {value: user.status});\n    }\n    return selected.length ? selected[0].text : \'Not set\';\n  };\n\n  $scope.checkName = function(data) {\n    if (data !== \'awesome\') {\n      return "Username should be `awesome`";\n    }\n  };\n\n  $scope.saveColumn = function(column) {\n    var results = [];\n    angular.forEach($scope.users, function(user) {\n      results.push($http.post(\'/saveColumn\', {column: column, value: user[column], id: user.id}));\n    })\n    return $q.all(results);\n  };\n\n});\n      </script>\n      <h3>\n       html\n <button class="btn btn-default" ng-click="tableform.$show()" ng-show="!tableform.$visible" type="button">\n           edit\n          </button>\n         </div>\n         <div class="btn-form ng-hide" ng-show="tableform.$visible">\n          <button class="btn btn-default pull-right" ng-click="addUser()" ng-disabled="tableform.$waiting" type="button">\n           add row\n          </button>\n          <button class="btn btn-primary" ng-disabled="tableform.$waiting" type="submit">\n           save\n          </button>\n          <button class="btn btn-default" ng-click="tableform.$cancel()" ng-disabled="tableform.$waiting" type="button">\n           cancel\n          </button>\n         </div>\n        </form>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Just wrap the whole table into\n       <code>\n        &lt;form&gt;\n       </code>\n       tag with\n       <code>\n        editable-form\n       </code>\n       attribute.\nNote that using\n       <code>\n        oncancel\n       </code>\n       hook allows you to revert all changes and put table into original state.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <!--script(src=dir+\'/controller.js\')-->\n      <script>\n       app.controller(\'EditableTableCtrl\', function($scope, $filter, $http, $q) {\n  $scope.users = [\n    {id: 1, name: \'awesome user1\', status: 2, group: 4, groupName: \'admin\'},\n    {id: 2, name: \'awesome user2\', status: undefined, group: 3, groupName: \'vip\'},\n    {id: 3, name: \'awesome user3\', status: 2, group: null}\n  ]; \n\n  $scope.statuses = [\n    {value: 1, text: \'status1\'},\n    {value: 2, text: \'status2\'},\n    {value: 3, text: \'status3\'},\n    {value: 4, text: \'status4\'}\n  ]; \n\n  $scope.groups = [];\n  $scope.loadGroups = function() {\n    return $scope.groups.length ? null : $http.get(\'/groups\').success(function(data) {\n      $scope.groups = data;\n    });\n  };\n\n  $scope.showGroup = function(user) {\n    if(user.group && $scope.groups.length) {\n      var selected = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.groups, {id: user.group});\n      return selected.length ? selected[0].text : \'Not set\';\n    } else {\n      return user.groupName || \'Not set\';\n    }\n  };\n\n  $scope.showStatus = function(user) {\n    var selected = [];\n    if(user.status) {\n      selected = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.statuses, {value: user.status});\n    }\n    return selected.length ? selected[0].text : \'Not set\';\n  };\n\n  $scope.checkName = function(data, id) {\n    if (id === 2 && data !== \'awesome\') {\n      return "Username 2 should be `awesome`";\n    }\n  };\n\n  // filter users to show\n  $scope.filterUser = function(user) {\n    return user.isDeleted !== true;\n  };\n\n  // mark user as deleted\n  $scope.deleteUser = function(id) {\n    var filtered = $filter(\'filter\')($scope.users, {id: id});\n    if (filtered.length) {\n      filtered[0].isDeleted = true;\n    }\n  };\n\n  // add user\n  $scope.addUser = function() {\n    $scope.users.push({\n      id: $scope.users.length+1,\n      name: \'\',\n      status: null,\n      group: null,\n      isNew: true\n    });\n  };\n\n  // cancel all changes\n  $scope.cancel = function() {\n    for (var i = $scope.users.length; i--;) {\n      var user = $scope.users[i];    \n      // undelete\n      if (user.isDeleted) {\n        delete user.isDeleted;\n      }\n      // remove new \n      if (user.isNew) {\n        $scope.users.splice(i, 1);\n      }      \n    };\n  };\n\n  // save edits\n  $scope.saveTable = function() {\n    var results = [];\n    for (var i = $scope.users.length; i--;) {\n      var user = $scope.users[i];\n      // actually delete user\n      if (user.isDeleted) {\n        $scope.users.splice(i, 1);\n      }\n      // mark as not new \n      if (user.isNew) {\n        user.isNew = false;\n      }\n\n      // send on server\n      results.push($http.post(\'/saveUser\', user));      \n    }\n\n    return $q.all(results);\n  };\n});\n      </script>\n      <h3>\n       html\n      </h3>\n      <pre class="prettyprint ng-non-bindable prettyprinted" style=""><span </section>\n     <h2>\n      Reference: editable element\n     </h2>\n     <h3>\n      Attributes\n     </h3>\n     <p>\n      Attributes can be defined for any element having\n      <code>\n     blur\n         </code>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         string\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <p>\n          Action when control losses focus. Values:\n          <code>\n           cancel|submit|ignore\n          </code>\n          .\nHas sense only for single editable element.\nOtherwise, if control is part of form - you should set\n          <code>\n           blur\n          </code>\n          of form, not of individual element.\n         </p>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <code>\n          buttons\n         </code>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         string\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <p>\n          Whether to show ok/cancel buttons. Values:\n          <code>\n           right|no\n          </code>\n          .\nIf set to\n          <code>\n           no\n          </code>\n          control automatically submitted when value changed.\n          <br/>\n          If control is part of form buttons will never be shown.\n         </p>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <code>\n          e-*\n         </code>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         any\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <p>\n          Attributes defined with\n          <code>\n           e-*\n          </code>\n          prefix automatically transferred from original element to\ncontrol.\n          <br/>\n          For example, if you set\n          <code>\n           &lt;span editable-text="user.name" e-style="width: 100px"\n          </code>\n          &gt;\nthen input will appear as\n          <code>\n           &lt;input style="width: 100px"&gt;\n          </code>\n          .\n          <br/>\n          See\n          <a href="#text-customize">\n           demo\n          </a>\n          .\n         </p>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <code>\n          onaftersave\n         </code>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         method\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <p>\n          Called during submit after value is saved to model.\n          <br/>\n          See\n          <a href="#onaftersave">\n           demo\n          </a>\n          .\n         </p>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <code>\n          onbeforesave\n         </code>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         method\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <p>\n          Called during submit before value is saved to model.\n          <br/>\n          See\n          <a href="#onbeforesave">\n           demo\n          </a>\n          .\n         </p>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <code>\n          oncancel\n         </code>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         method\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <p>\n          Called when control is cancelled.\n         </p>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <code>\n          onhide\n         </code>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         method\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <p>\n          Called when control is hidden after      Methods\n     </h3>\n     <p>\n      Methods are available when you set\n      <code>\n       name\n      </code>\n      attribute of form:\n     </p>\n     <pre class="prettyprint prettyprinted"      <th>\n         Description\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n      </thead>\n      <tbody>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <code>\n          $activate(name)\n         </code>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <strong>\n          name\n         </strong>\n         <i>\n          (string)\n         </i>\n         name of field\n         <br/>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <p>\n          Sets focus on form field specified by\n          <code>\n           name\n          </code>\n          .\n          <br/>\n          When trying to set the focus on a form field of a new row in
